Local News

Bureau of Public Works Report 49

Work on Reorganizing the War Zone

Damage Reaches 40 to 60 Percent

Property Damage Valued at Over 36 Million Yuan

Due to the impact of the war in the areas of Zhabei, Wusong, Jiangwan, and Zhenru in our city, various municipal construction projects have suffered significant damage. In light of this, the Bureau of Public Works has been actively involved in reorganization since the Japanese troops withdrew. The reorganization is now largely complete. Yesterday, the bureau issued a comprehensive report on the work of reorganizing the war zone. The details are copied below:

Since the Japanese army began its withdrawal on May 16th, our side took over the area south of the Songhu Railway and north of the Suzhou River. Subsequently, on May 23rd, we took over Zhenru Town and the area north of the Songhu Railway and west of Yokohama Road. On May 27th, we took over the central districts of Wusong and Jiangwan. However, the area east of the Songhu Railway and west of the Shajing River was not handed over until June 17th. As for the so-called "D Zone," west of the Songhu Railway and east of Yokohama Road, the Japanese army refused to withdraw, and only after more than a month of negotiations was it handed over on July 18th. The first step in the work of the bureau upon taking over was to quickly restore traffic on the roads in the war zone. The area south of the railway was less affected by the fire and was easier to reorganize. The area north of the railway was the center of the war. For example, in the area east of Song Park Road and north of Qiujiang Road, all the houses were destroyed by fire, and none survived. The roads were covered with rubble, some as thick as two meters. Defensive works such as trenches and sandbags were everywhere, especially in the area around Baoshan Road and West Baoxing Road. The road surface was damaged, and the ditches were blocked. The bridges on Yokohama Road were all destroyed. The towns of Wusong and Jiangwan suffered particularly heavy artillery fire, with houses reduced to ruins and scenes of devastation everywhere. Workers were dispatched to clear rubble, fill in trenches, demolish defensive works and dangerous walls, repair roads, clear ditches, and repair bridges to facilitate traffic. Other areas, such as Zhabei Jiaotong Road, Hutai Road, the Jungong Road along the Pu River, and the main roads in the city center, were also severely damaged. Because the regular workforce was insufficient, temporary workers were hired to speed up the repairs. All areas were cleaned up and traffic was unhindered within a few days of takeover. In addition, the Zhenxiang Road and Zhenbei Road, which were built during the war, were also filled with roadbeds and covered with coal cinder. According to statistics, 60% of the roads in the war zone were damaged, 40% of the canals were damaged and silted up, and 50% of the bridges were destroyed. In addition, most of the sidewalks and curbs were cracked by fire and explosions, and many street trees and street signs were also demolished. The scale of the losses is truly shocking and cannot be restored in a short period of time with limited funds. Therefore, the bureau had to weigh the urgency and prioritize reorganization. From May 16th to the end of July, a total of two and a half months, regular workers, temporary workers, and contractors were hired to step up their work, with a total of more than 40,000 workers engaged in the reorganization of roads, bridges, and other projects. The important achievements are as follows: A. Repaired asphalt road surfaces, including Datong Road, Hengfeng Road, Xinjiang Road, Baoshan Road, Guangdong Street, XinJia Road, Changchun Road, Dixiwei Road, Xiangyin Road, and Wusong Wai Ma Road, totaling 9075 meters. B. Repaired small square stone pavement, including Guangfu Road and Wuzhen Road, totaling 1100 meters. C. Repaired macadam pavement, including Datong Road, Haichang Road, Changan Road, Jinling Road, Meiyuan Road, Xinmin Road, Xinjiang Road, Mongolia Road, Guangfu Road, Huaxing Road, Kulun Road, Minli Road, Manchuria Road, Baoshan Road, West Baoxing Road, Qiujiang Road, Baotong Road, Xiangshan Road, Gongxing Road, Hongxing Road, Baochang Road, Baoyuan Road, Chuan Gong Road, Gonghexin Road, Yongxing Road, Huiwen Road, Zhongxing Road, Tiantong'an Road, Zhonghua Xin Road, Qingyun Road, Huachang Road, Wangjiazhaizhai Road, Tongge Road, Yokohama Road, Tongji Road, Huayuan Street, Zhongzhou Road, Guangdong Street, Jiangwan Road, Hengye Road, Jiaotong Road, Tehua Road, Tianbao Road, Linping Road, Xiangyanqiao Road, Xingjiaqiao Road, Hujiamuqiao Road, Xinjiade Run Road, Dongsheng Road, Shahong Road, and Wusong Wai Ma Road, totaling 38,025 meters. D. Repaired coal cinder pavement, including Datong Road, Baochang Road, Gonghexin Road, Yongxing Road, Zhongxing Road, Zhonghua Xin Road, Huachang Road, Song Park Road, Jinshan Road, Changxing Road, Xinma Road, Jiangwan Road, Jiaotong Road, Hutai Road, Zhongshan South Road, Zhongshan North Road, Liuying Road, North Baoxing Road, Yuexiu Road, Lingnan Road, Gu Chang Road, Tianbao Road, Quanjia'an Road, Ouyang Road, Xiangde Road, Huacheng Road, Tongjia Road, Changchun Road, Nanshan Road, Shuidian Road, Xinshi Road, Lida Road, East Tiyu Hui Road, Mayushan Road, Huangxing Road, Zhijiang Road, Xiangyin Road, Songhu Road, Zhayin Road, Tengpei Road, Guanyintang Road, Yinxing Road, Chezhanxi Road, Sanmin Road, Wuquan Road, Jungong Road, Chunjiang Road, Paotaiwan, Wusong Tongji Road, Wusong Wai Ma Road, Zhenxiang Road, Zhenru Sanmin Road, and Zhenru Chezhan Road, totaling 95,375 meters. E. Repaired bridges, including Gongxing Bridge, Liuying Bridge, Pushan Bridge, Xiaoyang Bridge, Yangjia Bridge, Zuoshi

Ziqiao Bridge, Wuzhen Bridge, Hengfeng Bridge, Baoshan Road Yokohama Bridge, East Tiyu Hui Road Shajinggang Bridge, Qimei Road Shajinggang Bridge, Shuidian Road Shajinggang Bridge, Xiangyin Road No. 2 Bridge, Songhu Road No. 2 Bridge, Songhu Road No. 1 Bridge, Sanmin Wuquan Road No. 3 Bridge, Yinxing Road Hujia Bridge, Yuexiu Road No. 1 Bridge, Yuexiu Road No. 2 Bridge, Yuexiu Road No. 3 Bridge, Yinxiang Hujiamuqiao Bridge, Yinxiang Fenshuimiao Bridge, Zhongshan Road No. 1 Bridge, Zhongshan Road No. 4 Bridge, F. Repaired ditch pipes 114 meters, repaired skylights 13, repaired gullies 15, G. Repaired double-sided right 86 meters, repaired cement sidewalks 187 square meters, H. Replenished street trees and branches around the trees 3,898, I. Cleared rubble from various roads, transported sandbags and defensive structures, and filled in trenches, totaling 13,380 cubic meters. As for the area of ​​houses destroyed within the war zone, a total of six districts including Zhabei, Wusong, Yinxiang, Jiangwan, Pengpu, and Zhenru, is about 740,000 square meters, and the area of ​​damaged houses is about 19,000 square meters, totaling 930,000 square meters. It is estimated that the loss should be more than 36 million yuan. After the war, the devastation has not yet recovered, and residents have nowhere to live. Therefore, the Bureau immediately stipulated that the exemption of construction and repair permits would be for three months, and other procedures were reduced as much as possible in order to facilitate. From the cessation of the war to the end of August, a total of 583 free construction permits were issued in the war zone, accounting for approximately 79,000 square meters, which is only slightly more than one-tenth of the destroyed area. The estimated construction value is approximately 920,000 yuan, and 283 repair permits and 170 miscellaneous permits have been issued. This is the situation of the reorganization in terms of construction. At the beginning of the takeover, the Engineering Management Office of Zhabei Minli Road was occupied by the pseudo-Shanghai Northern People's Local Maintenance Association, and all stationery and sundries were searched and emptied, and the books, charts, and tables were torn and messy. The situation of the Changchun Road Workshop and the Xiangyin Road Engineering Management Office in the city center was also the same. The loss of materials and tools is valued at more than 35,000 yuan. In addition, when sandbags were removed from Baoshan Road, Baoxing Road, and other places, 55 abandoned hand-held grenades, 12 bombs, 16 large and small artillery shells, and 3,371 rounds of bullets were found one after another, and they were sent to the Shanghai North Office of the Public Security Bureau and various districts for storage. All offices have now been restored to their original state and are operating as usual, and dangerous objects in the roads have also been removed. This is an incident of incidental reorganization. According to this bureau, the funds for handling the aftermath of the war zone were approved by the municipal government and allocated 100,000 yuan, but only 50,000 yuan was received by September 12, so the above-mentioned projects such as roads, ditches, and bridges were only reorganized selectively within the scope of possible funds. There are still many projects that need to be repaired in the war zone, and they cannot be carried out until the municipal government continues to allocate funds. In addition, houses in Wusong, Jiangwan, and Zhabei have been built one after another after the war, and they have all been acquired in accordance with the established road plan, but the road surface after the acquisition, as well as the ditches under the road, have not been paved due to lack of funds, and the citizens are very strict in supervising this, so funds should be raised as soon as possible to start construction as soon as possible to comfort those who are expecting it.

Public Security Bureau Detective Team 50

Kidnapping Case Solved in Xiaoshan

Young Hostage Safely Rescued

The Victim's Cousin Masterminded the Crime

Detectives Were Extremely Brave

Six Male and Female Bandits Were Captured One After Another

Dai Wenzhi, courtesy name Zibin, is 37 years old and is from Tiantai Mountain in Zhejiang Province. He is currently working as an accountant at the Yuantai Coal Company established by Liu Hongsheng, a major real estate merchant at No. 6 Sichuan Road. He lives at No. 10 Xicang Lane, Xicang Street, inside Laolao Ximen in Nanshi. Dai is thrifty by nature, and his family is quite wealthy. Unexpectedly, he was coveted by bandits. Dai has a young son named Along, who is only five years old. The bandits learned that Dai loved this son like the apple of his eye, so at about 2 pm on August 20th of this year, they kidnapped Along at the gate of Dai's house. At that time, Dai did not report to the police station rashly out of fear, and ordered his family to keep the secret strictly, not to make any noise, hoping to give the bandits a chance to contact him. Unexpectedly, the bandits' hopes were too extravagant, and they demanded a ransom of 100,000 yuan. A total of five letters were received from the bandits, and the family sent people to contact them three times, but the bandits still insisted on a minimum of 70,000 yuan. Until recently, there were still no results. Dai had no choice but to report to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. After a thorough investigation by Detective Captain Lu Ying, multiple kidnappers in this case were arrested around 11 pm the night before, and the hostage was safely rescued from the bandit's lair. The details are recorded below.

Appointed Time for Negotiation Since Along was kidnapped on August 20th of this year, there has been no news for a full week. On August 28th, the bandits contacted the victim, Dai Wenzhi, for the first time to meet in person at Yaojia Zhushao Xing to negotiate. At that time, Dai was afraid that the bandits would trick him into going and that it would be dangerous, so he did not go. The second time, the bandits sent a letter to Dai asking him to contact him near the Waibaidu Bridge at 3 pm on the 9th of this month. Dai secretly reported to Captain Lu, who immediately sent the foreman Shan Bin, along with detectives Chen Liangfu and others, to join the constables disguised as civilians to go to the scene with the victim to wait for the bandits. However, the bandits did not arrive, so it was ineffective.

Yuyao Contacted Until the third time, the kidnappers suddenly sent another letter asking him to go to the Wufu Railway Station in Yuyao from 11 am to 1 pm on the 13th to negotiate. The letter stated that the visitor must hold three cans of "Beautiful" brand cigarettes and a towel as a sign. After receiving the report, Captain Lu sent the foreman Shan Bin, along with the original detectives, from Shanghai to Hangzhou on the 12th, and then to Wufu Railway Station. At that time, Shan foreman and the victim exchanged clothes and waited near the platform track. The other detectives were ambushed all around, waiting for the bandits to come.

Two Bandits Captured Immediately At 11:15 am, a bandit with a pockmarked face wearing a yuan-colored gown walked slowly. Speaking with a northern accent, he grabbed the left wrist of the Shan foreman and said, "Let's go up the mountain and talk about it in detail," and put one hand into his pocket to pretend to hold a gun. Shan immediately said, "You can talk here." After walking about five or six steps shoulder to shoulder, Shan suddenly flashed back, tightly hugging the bandit. After struggling, he was finally overwhelmed by the detectives and captured. At that time, the victim's brother, Dai Wenrui, had already spotted a bandit who came with him and chased him down.

One Bandit Captured in Shanghai After the two bandits were captured, they were sent to the Yuyao County Public Security Bureau. After a preliminary interrogation, the bandit who was captured first confessed his name was Jin Tianyun, from Sheng County, 29 years old. The bandit who was captured later confessed his name was Zhang Zibing, from Sheng County, 33 years old, who used to work in the Yunlun Silk Factory in Xiaocai Chang, Yongxing Road, Zhabei. He confessed that Ma Huanlao, who hid in the front building on the second floor of Wufuli No. 6, Meiyuan Road, Gonghe Road, Zhabei, Shanghai, sent the hostage to hide in the countryside of Xiaoshan, Shaoxing. Upon hearing this confession, Shan foreman immediately telegraphed Captain Lu, who sent the foreman Liu Shaoqing to go to the address with the Fourth District Chief Police at 12:00 that night and arrested Ma. The Hostage Out of Danger After Ma was arrested, he was taken to the team for strict interrogation. According to his confession, the hostage had indeed been sent to Xiaoshan for hiding. Captain Lu then sent additional detectives to accompany the original staff and the victim to Xiaoshan. At 11 pm the night before, the detective team had received a telegram report from Xiaoshan, saying that the hostage Dai Along had been safely rescued and two male and one female bandits had been arrested. However, one of them who confessed his name was Dai Wenqing, was the victim's cousin. However, Wenqing's brother, Dai Wenbiao, had already escaped upon hearing the news. At 3:30 pm yesterday, Shan foreman and others had escorted the hostage and the bandits to Shanghai. Captain Lu then reported to the director for review.

Assassination Case on Guling Road 51

The Murderer Was Arrested on the Spot

The Perpetrator Strenuously Refused to Confess

At around 8:30 yesterday morning, a man wearing a black Indian silk gown was running wildly from west to east on Guling Road. Behind him, another man who looked like a worker was holding a knife and chasing closely. When the man ran to the entrance of the Da Cifu Hotel, he tripped and fell to the ground because a rickshaw was parked in front of him. The worker immediately caught up, stabbing the man several times in the chest and throat with a sharp blade, and then discarded the blade and fled towards Xizang Road. At that time, a man surnamed Dai happened to be passing by and shouted "Murder!" which was heard by the guards nearby. They chased and arrested the murderer, picked up the murder weapon, and took them to the Old Zhabei Police Station along with the witness surnamed Dai. The police station immediately sent detectives to the scene to investigate and transported the body to the Fielun Road Morgue for examination. Then, the police station interrogated the murderer, who confessed his name was Zhang Zimei, from Tongzhou, 30 years old, living at No. 374 Kangnaiduo Road, and worked as a rickshaw puller. He strenuously refused to confess to the murder, so the police station still needs to conduct a strict interrogation.

Tonghua Has Not Yet Emerged from Shoal 52

The Tonghua ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ran aground at Huangsangkou, Qizhou. The bow of the ship was stuck in the sand. Initially, the Lijitunan two ships were sent to tow it, but Tunan's military transport was tight and it was inconvenient to help tow. Therefore, the Lijitunan was weak and unable to rescue it, and the Tonghua's bow was stuck in the sand, which was quite dangerous. Yesterday, the chief captain of the bureau personally went to Huangsangkou to investigate, and ordered the Jiangxin ship to depart at noon yesterday to assist in towing. According to Wang Tong, the director of the shipping department, the tide was expected to rise yesterday afternoon, and it was hoped that the towing would be successful.

Postal Inspection Office 53

Director Xu Unreasonably Assaults Postal Worker

The Postal Administration of the North Sichuan Road Postal Administration in this port has a postal inspection office stationed there, with more than 20 inspectors. They work in shifts every day, inspecting reactionary mail in various post office rooms. Yesterday morning, the director of the office, Xu Zhenliu, was taking the stairs to go upstairs, accidentally touched the elevator door machine, suspected that the machine was deliberately treating him badly, and was instantly furious. He beat the driver, Li. Li reported to the postmaster that the officer had assaulted him for no reason, and that the officer was the director of the postal inspection office, but had such barbaric behavior. Xu not only did not admit his mistake, but was also strong and insisted that Li was disrespectful to him and deserved to be beaten. Later, the whole postal workers heard about this matter, and all were resentful of Xu's arrogant and bullying attitude towards postal workers. It is said that the postal authorities believe that a postal civil servant was unreasonably beaten, and have made serious representations to the competent authority of the office.

County Defense Committee Congress 55

Seventh Session

The Shanghai County Defense Committee held its seventh congress at the County Government Conference Room at 10 am yesterday. All committee members, heads of various districts, and chiefs of various districts were present. The meeting was chaired by Deputy Chairman Qin Yanqi, and the minutes were recorded by Hu Bochang. The meeting began as usual. First, Xu Yi, Director of the Office, reported on the progress of the special training class in the past two months. Then, the resolutions were discussed and decided. (1) It is proposed to appropriately extend the period for which the special training class of the Defense Regiment of this county is held by one month. The resolution was passed according to the original proposal. (2) The head of the Fourth District proposed to allocate the defense funds accumulated by the Production Department to settle the arrears before the 21st year. The resolution was, the arrears of each district before the 21st year will be compensated by the surplus funds before the 21st year. From the 21st year, the budget will be collected and spent, and there will be no more arrears. (3) The head of the First District suggested establishing a district defense committee. The resolution was, the First District will supplement the reasons and submit them to the county to be forwarded to the provincial capital for review.

Qian Miaofu Kidnapping Case: Kidnappers Sentenced 56

Qian Guan Jin's seven-year-old only son, Miaofu, who lived at No. 7, Lane 206, Pu'en Jishi Road, French Concession, was suddenly kidnapped and hidden while enjoying the cool in the patio at 7 pm on July 20th of this year. A huge ransom was demanded. Jin Jiulin, detective inspector of the special agency of the French Police Station, and detectives Li Yaolong and Zhang Ziying, and the patrol detectives, arrested the kidnappers Wei Youwen, Wang Shaoqing, and Xu Dashunzi from Jiangbei, and rescued the hostage on a small boat in the river at the bottom of Haige Road and escorted him home. After the police station completed the investigation, Wei and others were sent to the Second Special Zone District Court for public prosecution. Court President Wang Gangxu repeatedly held court to study the case, and designated two lawyers, Wang Shizong and Shen Yushan, to defend the defendants. The final debate has been declared, and the verdict is pending. Yesterday was the date of the verdict. At 10 am, Court President Wang, accompanied by Secretary Ren Qiyuan, arrived at the Criminal Court and ordered the defendants to be brought to court. Wei Youwen and Wang Shaoqing were sentenced to six years of imprisonment each for the crime of conspiring to kidnap and extort ransom, and deprived of their civil rights for five years. Xu Dashunzi was sentenced to life imprisonment for the crime of jointly kidnapping and extorting ransom and deprived of his civil rights for life. One bullet was confiscated. After the sentence, the defendants were still returned to prison to await the expiration of the appeal period before being sent to prison for execution.

Girl Falls in Love with Beat Cop 57

Not Ashamed of His Low Status

Only Loves His Excellent Character

Xi Huiyun, the 18-year-old daughter of Xi Zixiang, who lives at No. 109, Furun Lane, Nine Mu Di, in the city, is very beautiful and graduated from Wanzhu Primary School. She is currently studying at Jinde Junior High School. Unexpectedly, she fell in love with the patrol officer Ni Shizhong (25 years old) of the Second District, First Station, Yangzhou. An old woman, Xu Yan, introduced a small house to them at the Tang Feng's house at No. 2, Jiujian Lou, Qiaojia Bang, and Huiyun eloped and left home. Later, her father sent out detectives to find Huiyun first, asked about the previous situation, and also arrested the police officer, together with Xu Yan and others, and twisted them into the Third Station of the First District. During the interrogation, Xi Huiyun claimed that the love was real, but she had asked Ni to break off the relationship, and this time she was coerced into abduction, etc. They were immediately escorted to the Public Security Bureau and transferred to the District Court yesterday. The prosecutor conducted a preliminary hearing, and Huiyun said that when she began to fall in love with Ni, during the summer when they were cooling off, his post was in front of the door, and they loved each other and became lovers. "I am not ashamed of his low status, I love his excellent character. I agreed to borrow a small house to escape, and what I said before was listening to Qian Alin's words, and my father also listened to Qian Alin's words to destroy our good deeds," etc. When questioned about Ni Shizhong, his confession was also similar. Xu Yan's confession was vague. The official ordered them to be detained together, waiting for the informant to arrive for further handling.

Organized Stone Throwing Agency

Three Abducted Children Rescued

Lu Gendi, Ding Huaguo, Sun Jishan, and other Chinese detectives of the Xinzha Police Station, learned that there were Fujian gang members organizing a stone-throwing agency (i.e., a cut for trafficking in young boys) at No. 1144, Tongchun Lane, Gongping Road, who specialized in buying children and reselling them to Fuzhou and other places to make a profit. Sanitary Inspector's Extortion Exposed 59

Accused of Negligence of Duty and Obtaining Property by Fraud

Qian Guisheng, a sanitary inspector from Pingliang Road Works Bureau and a native of this county, went to the vendors of the Wuzhou Road Xiaocai Chang from the 5th to the 9th of this month at around 2 pm, pretending to be instructed by foreigners to move the noodle stalls and other 13 households to the second floor for business. Because the upper floor has no roof and is open-air, customers are inconvenient and no one patronizes. They begged him to find a way to ban it, and Qian asked for 300 yuan. As a result, 250 yuan was negotiated. Because one of the households could not raise enough money, it fell short of 28 yuan, which was all taken away by Qian, indicating that they could still live in the old place. Unexpectedly, the chief foreigner of the sanitation department received an anonymous letter in Western text the day before, stating the above facts, and since there was no such move in the bureau, Qian Guisheng was sent to the Jiaxing Road Police Station and detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Fourth Criminal Court of the First Special Zone. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated the previous situation, claiming that the police accused the defendant of negligence of duty and obtaining property by fraud, please investigate. Now all the stallholders have arrived in court, etc. According to Zhang Zigui's statement, he set up a noodle stall on the lower floor of the Xiaocai Chang. The defendant came to tell him that it was unsanitary and needed to be moved to the upper floor for business. When he discussed with him, he attributed it to the foreigner and wanted 300 yuan. After repeated negotiations, the stallholders gathered 222 yuan and handed it over to the defendant for counting on the second floor of the Xiaocai Chang. He claimed that there was still a shortage that must be made up, and then took the money away, etc. According to the woman Wang Houshi, who is also a noodle stall vendor, her testimony was the same as Zhang's, and she also claimed that there was a shortage of 28 yuan because Yan Laigen, one household, did not pay, etc. According to Yan's claim, the defendant said that it was foreigners who wanted the money, not him, and he did not get any of it because he had no money. Questioning the defendant's confession, the money was all taken away by the Western staff member named Nkon, and he did not get any of it. The Westerner is going somewhere on the 11th and is expected to return in about a week. The rest of his confession was vague. Prosecutor Fu Lin ordered him to be returned to custody, and the hearing was postponed to wait for the Westerner to arrive for questioning.

Judgment for Embezzlement of Printing Costs 60

The Henan Provincial Geological Survey recently commissioned the Shanghai Yuanfeng Printing Company to print 500 copies of a report. After accepting the commission, the company intended to subcontract the printing to another printing house. Therefore, they instructed their salesman, Ye Weiru, to contact other printing houses. Ye then claimed that the printing had been undertaken by the Meihua Printing House, and Yuanfeng accordingly gave Ye 680 yuan to be forwarded to Meihua as printing fees. Later, as the agreed deadline passed and Meihua still had not delivered the goods, Yuanfeng contacted Meihua regarding the order and discovered that Ye had been lying. The money had been entirely used by Ye for his own purposes. The matter was reported to the police, who dispatched detectives to arrest Ye. Yesterday, he was brought before Chief Judge Qian of the First Special District Court. Ye confessed that he had used the money for funeral expenses, but claimed that the report was already in the process of being printed, and only a slight extension of time was needed. Defendant's lawyer, Yan Luqing, defended the defendant, requesting leniency. Judge Qian concluded the interrogation and immediately pronounced judgment, sentencing Ye Weiru to three months of imprisonment as a warning.

Xu Yucheng's Response 61

to the Indictment for Property Encroachment

Xu Yucheng, a shareholder of Hengtong Qianzhuang, was sued by his nephews, Wenrong and Wenxin, who together retained lawyer E Sen, for encroaching on jointly owned public property under his management. The case was once heard in the First Special District Court. The court ruled that the accounts submitted by the defendant required further examination and ordered further investigation. This has been reported in the newspapers. Now, the defendant has entrusted his lawyers, Yang Linzhi and Ye Shaoying, to submit a statement detailing the management situation over the years, and has also filed a counterclaim. The statement roughly states: "My late father, Xiaoyun, had three sons: the eldest, Shiming (deceased, father of the plaintiff Wenrong), the second, Shizhong (Yucheng), and the youngest, Shiheng (deceased, father of Wenxin). Their estate was divided in the 31st year of the Guangxu reign (1905), with written records as proof. At that time, my late mother, Lady Zha, was still alive, so my late father's

Page 12

estate was divided into four portions. The three remaining sons each received one portion, and the remaining portion was reserved as public property for the expenses of my mother during her lifetime, for her funeral arrangements after her death, and for other public expenses. In the eighth month of the 32nd year of the Guangxu reign (1906), I, Yucheng, was working in Beijing. The aforementioned public property was managed by Shiheng for four years and two months. In the tenth month of the second year of the Xuantong reign (1910), Shiheng passed away. I, Yucheng, returned from Beijing to my hometown to audit the public accounts of my deceased brother, and found a deficit of over 1,000 yuan. In the third month of the third year of the Xuantong reign (1911), I, Yucheng, requested leave to care for my elderly mother as I was the only able-bodied son at home. I also returned to the south to make arrangements for a memorial hall to be built for my late father in Beijing. Therefore, the public accounts were handed over to Menghua for management (Menghua is the elder brother of Wenrong). In the ninth month, I returned south and found a deficit of several hundred yuan in the public accounts. It was then that the Xinhai Revolution occurred and the family fled to Shanghai for safety. The second month after that was the first year of the Republic (1912), and it was then that I, Yucheng, began to manage the public property together with the members of each branch of the family. Upon investigation, the income of the public account was originally not much. After moving to Shanghai, expenses increased sharply. The rent and rice expenses for each branch of the family were all paid from the public account. Since April of the fourth year of the Republic (1915), each branch of the family paid for their own rent and rice. My late mother, Lady Zha, was over seventy years old, and we dared not be frugal in providing for her. The plaintiffs lived with my late mother in Shanghai, but did not know that all expenses were paid from the public account. This is the situation of the public accounts from the first year of the Republic (1912) to the twelfth year of the Republic (1923). The expenses for my late mother's birthdays and funeral arrangements are all recorded in the account books and can be easily verified. After my late mother passed away, the expenses of the public accounts decreased. I, Yucheng, following my late mother's wishes, allocated 600 shi of paddy land rental from Pinghu to her eldest and second grandsons, valued at 20,000 yuan. In addition to the above, the income and expenses over the years are all supported by detailed account statements. Except that the plaintiffs have taken away three account books and refused to return them, making it impossible to complete the final accounting, all other account documents have been audited and categorized by accountant Wang Sifang, listing everything without omission. I, Yucheng, am over sixty years old and suffer from many illnesses, making it difficult for me to write and calculate. It is unavoidable that things have piled up, but the management of public accounts is a completely unpaid service. I dare not hire an accountant, and each branch of the family should understand this. Moreover, the plaintiffs and I are akin to father and nephews, and if they had any conscience or knew even the most basic etiquette, they could have directly investigated the accounts or convened a family meeting. Why resort to litigation in the public court over the estate of our ancestors? Furthermore, the plaintiffs stated in their complaint that from the twelfth year of the Republic (1923) to the twentieth year of the Republic (1931), the interest on pledges and the remittance of rents and land taxes to Yucheng amounted to a total of 55,929 yuan, 3 jiao, 9 fen, and 5 li. After deducting the expenses of the Haiyan Accounting Office and the public accounts, there should still be 39,912 yuan and 3 jiao in savings. However, after my late mother passed away, the expenses for her funeral arrangements alone amounted to over 16,200 yuan, which the plaintiffs ignored, writing it off with a stroke of the pen. It is heartbreaking to speak of this. They also claim that I, Yucheng, cannot point out where such a large sum of money is deposited, and that the accounts are also missing, using this as evidence of my embezzlement, which cannot be refuted. How can they not know that the accounts I handed over, covering the period from the twelfth year of the Republic (1923) to the twentieth year of the Republic (1931), show that the amount received was 74,178 yuan, 1 jiao, and 6 li, which exceeds the amount mentioned by the plaintiffs by over 20,000 yuan? This shows that the plaintiffs are not clear about the amount of income and recklessly accuse others of embezzlement. Their slander and framing are self-evident. Furthermore, if I, Yucheng, had any intention of embezzling, why would I admit to receiving more than 20,000 yuan more? This alone is enough to prove my honesty and impartiality. I, Yucheng, have been reading books since childhood and have a basic understanding of etiquette. For decades, I have been dedicated to public affairs, and I know the difference between righteousness and profit. Not only have I never set foot in a public court, but I have also rarely had disputes with relatives and friends. Now, to be accused by my nephews of embezzling thousands upon thousands of yuan, of embezzling every minute detail, of having the ambition of Mount Tai not refusing any soil, and of the tolerance of the rivers and seas not discriminating against small streams, their intention is nothing more than to destroy me through condemnation. I, Yucheng, only have the virtue of walking alone, but lack the virtue of influencing others. In seeking the reasons within myself, I cannot face my ancestors in the afterlife. Thinking of this, I am filled with fear and remorse. I have separately compiled a detailed list of income and expenses over the years and request the court to verify them one by one. If there are any false reports, exaggerations, embezzlements for personal gain, I am willing to be severely punished to uphold the law and apologize to my ancestors." In the counterclaim, it is stated that he has only daughters and no sons. Recently, the National Government promulgated the law on women's inheritance of property. His two nephews have no hope of inheriting his property, so they are using the public account as a pretext to covet his property, making a fuss over a minor issue. It is obvious that their intention is to subject him to criminal penalties and to file a private prosecution. The plaintiffs have violated Article 180 and Article 181 of the Criminal Law regarding false accusations, without any doubt. Therefore, according to Article 365 of the Criminal Law, he is filing a counterclaim.

Letter to the Editor 76

Having read the report in your newspaper (15th) about the eye-gouging case of the Ding family, I am very shocked. I have been living in Zhabei, Shanghai, as a tailor. Last autumn, I brought my family back to my hometown and reclaimed the ancestral farmland for my own cultivation. Since then, I have incurred the resentment of my clan. This time, due to drying sorghum husks, I had a dispute with Ding Changxian. At first, I was beaten by a mob, and then both of my eyes were gouged out. I did not expect the villains to be so ruthless and have committed such a heinous crime. I have an elderly mother above me and a wife and children below me. My whole family relies on making a living. Now that I have suddenly lost my sight, my livelihood is cut off. As for the matter of not engaging in proper work and stealing clothing from the clan, which has damaged my reputation, I think your newspaper's report is inaccurate and should be corrected as soon as possible. I sincerely ask the gentlemen of the Shen Bao newspaper to take note. Yours truly, Ding Achun. September 15th, 21st year of the Republic.

Jiangsu Provincial Education College Conserves Funds to Aid Troops 80

The Patriotic Association of Faculty and Staff of Jiangsu Provincial Education College in Wuxi, in view of the lack of ammunition and supplies for the Northeastern Volunteer Army, and the lack of external support, could not bear to sit idly by while they fought on empty stomachs. City Education Bureau Orders 81

Commemoration of "September 18th"

Call for a Gathering of All Students at 9:00 AM

Suspend Regular Weekly Holidays and Lecture on Facts of National Humiliation

Yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued instructions to major private primary and secondary schools in the city, stating: "As per the Ministry of Education's telegraph, the one-year anniversary of the September 18th National Humiliation is approaching. The unprecedented humiliation is unforgettable. The disaster is still ongoing and is becoming more intense. All of us Chinese people are in pain and indignation every day, and especially on this day, we should actively encourage ourselves to be the vanguard for all sectors. For this purpose, all levels of schools across the country are ordered to convene all students in the school at 9:00 AM on this day to hold a commemoration, suspend regular weekly holidays, lecture on the facts of national humiliation, and discuss methods of saving the country, in order to demonstrate the spirit of perseverance and prepare to wipe out the humiliation and regain honor. All schools are instructed to strictly comply and instruct their subordinates to comply accordingly." This order is hereby issued for compliance.

Faculty and Staff Should Participate in Morning Exercises 83

Morning Exercises Can Be Changed to Class Exercises in Case of Difficulties

After Mr. Pan Gongzhan assumed the position of Director of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, he has paid extraordinary attention to physical education. The bureau specifically issued Instruction No. 27 on the previous day, notifying primary and secondary schools, stating: "Morning exercises at schools are very important. All teachers in each school should also participate in morning exercises uniformly and conduct them effectively in order to emphasize physical education. For schools with a large number of commuting students, if there are practical difficulties or those who cannot attend, they can be changed to class exercises. The time should be scheduled after the first or second period in the morning and must be included in the daily timetable starting this year, with two copies submitted for review two weeks before the start of school. It is hereby urgently ordered that all primary and secondary schools comply accordingly."

Physical Education

Painful Commemoration of September 18th 84

Should Stop Sports

The painful commemoration of the Northeast's fall on September 18th coincides with a Sunday. According to common practice, Sunday is a holiday, and sports competitions are more frequent than usual. However, this Sunday (September 18th) also has important advanced singles semi-finals in the grass tennis tournament. To commemorate the painful September 18th, all competitions under the auspices of the China National Sports Federation should be suspended. Moreover, for those presided over by Westerners, our compatriots should refrain from participating on that day. Mr. Qin Shouou, who is concerned about this matter, sent a letter, which is transcribed below. It is hoped that patriotic Chinese people will pay attention.

(Omitted above) I read in the newspaper that the singles semi-finals between Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai, and Zheng Zhaojia and Defu, will be held this Sunday at the French Chamber of Commerce. Upon investigation, this competition was originally scheduled for today, but the French Chamber of Commerce, for the sake of its income, specifically postponed it to Sunday. However, it has been found that Sunday happens to be the commemoration of "September 18th." The government has already issued a nationwide order to suspend entertainment. Since Lin, Qiu, and Zheng are Chinese, and tennis is also a form of entertainment, it is an undeniable fact that they should comply with the order to suspend the competition. I sincerely hope that your newspaper will publish an article opposing holding tennis matches on "September 18th" and ask you to inform other newspapers to advocate this position together. Your newspaper is enthusiastic about patriotism, and it must not be less than this humble person. I eagerly await this. Respectfully, Qin Shouou, September 15th.

Grass Tennis Doubles Championship 86

Lin and Qiu Enter the Finals Week

Although Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang Lost

Their Skillful Advancement Was Applauded by the Audience

| Defu and Huite Also Secure Final Rights |

The final of the Shanghai Grass Tennis Club's Doubles Championship saw Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai face Defu and Huite. The results of yesterday afternoon's semi-finals at the French Chamber of Commerce were: (1) Defu and Huite narrowly defeated Mei Hamsi and Beilunsi in five sets. (2) Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai defeated Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang in straight sets.

Encountering Strong Opponents, a Hard-Fought Victory

Defu and Huite, an unexpected strong opponent, confronted Beilunsi and Mei Hamsi, one tall and one short, one high and one low. They almost thwarted Defu and Huite's hopes of winning the championship. Beilunsi utilized his height, smashing everywhere, and his fast shots along the sidelines were especially accurate and powerful. Although Mei Hamsi was short, his net play was not inferior, and his high balls were also quite accurate and commendable. Their coordinated advances and retreats made the veterans sigh in admiration.

The Arena Resounded with Smashes The situation in this group was that both sides aimed to win by smashing. Beilunsi and Mei Hamsi exerted all their strength to smash, and they won two sets entirely due to this. Furthermore, Defu also excelled at this, so the entire arena resounded with smashes.

Strategic Error In the first set, Defu and Huite's balls were often out of bounds, coupled with the fierce smashes from Beilunsi and Mei Hamsi. After 2-2, Defu and Huite lost three consecutive games, trailing 2-5. Only then did they realize the error of trading smashes and switched to accurate high balls, winning back three games to tie at 5-5. However, at 7-6, they suddenly lost two more games. Finally, after many "equal" games, they won the first set 10-8.

Defu Shows His Colors Although Defu and Huite narrowly won the first set, they lost the second set 4-6 under the heavy pressure of their strong opponents. They tied at 4-4 and then lost two consecutive games. With each side winning one set, Defu displayed his colors in the third set, resuming his fierce and accurate net play and smashing, which was crisp, refreshing, and impressive. After 3-1, they relentlessly won three more games, winning the third set 6-1 and taking a 2-1 lead.

Impatience Leads to Failure However, things turned out unexpectedly. In the fourth set, Beilunsi and Mei Hamsi again tied the score at 2-2 with a 6-2 win. In the final decisive set, Beilunsi and Mei Hamsi failed due to impatience. Defu and Huite took a 3-2 lead. Mei Hamsi then lost a serve, putting them in a disadvantageous position. Subsequently, Defu and Huite rallied from 1-3 to win the set 5-2. In the final game, Beilunsi committed two double faults, practically handing over the victory.

The Veterans Won, but the Youngsters Showed Their Prowess

Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai 6-3, 6-1, 6-4 Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang

Although Lin and Qiu won in straight sets after a fierce battle, they had actually gone through a tough fight. In the third set, Zheng and Yu took a 4-3 lead, seemingly poised to win a set. However, in several games, Zheng and Yu had led 3-1 but were overtaken by Lin and Qiu.

Zheng Zhaojia Highly Praised Zheng Zhaojia's performance has shown a glimpse of his recent improvement in skills. His serves were heavy and powerful, and his shots demonstrated his ability to concentrate his power. His cross-court shots flew like arrows, and Lin and Qiu rarely returned them. His strategy was also good, using high balls to force Lin and Qiu back, all very accurate, especially in the third set.

Yu Tianguang's Weaknesses Yu Tianguang's performance yesterday can also be considered a brilliant one. Against such strong opponents, it should be judged differently. His shots were also powerful, and his net play was excellent. However, his weakness was his lack of courage. In the first two sets, his high balls were too close, all falling into Lin and Qiu's hands. However, he performed much better in the third set, with his heavy cross-court shots from the baseline often hitting inside the net. He should be further trained.

Score of the Re-Semi-Final Zheng and Yu defeated Tuina and Kelinuofu to gain re-semi-final rights, with a score of 14-12, 6-2, 6-2.

Mid-Autumn Festival 87

Donghua Heavily Defeats Lincoln

Seven Thousand Fans Are Overjoyed

Lincoln Suffers a Crushing Defeat 5-2

| Tragedy on the Field: Lincoln Player's Leg Bone Fractured |

Yesterday, the Donghua Football Team faced Lincoln with full spirit, and as a result, Donghua won a resounding victory with a score of 5-2, marking Lincoln's first defeat since arriving in Shanghai. Yesterday also coincided with the Mid-Autumn Festival, and various sectors were on holiday, so the attendance at the match was exceptionally enthusiastic, estimated to be over 7,000 people. The baseball field was completely filled, a rare sight. The performance was brilliant, and everyone who watched was overjoyed, adding much color to the auspicious day. However, the tragedy of Lincoln's left inside forward, Lix, breaking his leg bone was a blemish on the otherwise perfect day. The details are described below.

Donghua Excels in Both Offense and Defense Donghua's defenders cooperated well. Feng Yunyou marked Lincoln's center forward, Tu Kaiyuan guarded the tiger general Kou Kehanmu closely, Wu Youliang marked the left-wing, Li Ning and Guan Xun'an marked the two inside forwards, and Lu Zhongen defended the goal. Everyone performed their duties and was well-prepared and impeccable. The short passes of the forwards Chen Jiaqiu and Chen Yutian were extremely skillful, making it impossible for the opponent to predict. Qian Jingyong was as brave as ever and made many wonderful passes, contributing greatly. Cao Qiulin's shooting was strong, but he was too timid. In summary, the whole team was energetic and full of vigor, but the performance was slightly slow. The lineup was as follows:

Lu Zhongen, Li Ning, Guan Xun'an (Wang Changying replaced him), Tu Kaiyuan, Feng Yunyou, Wu Youliang, Qian Jingyong, Wan Xianghua (Chen Hongguang replaced him), Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Yutian, Cao Qiuting

Lincoln's Lineup Has Adjustments Lincoln's lineup was slightly different from the first match. The famous general Barnes Pei did not play, and Lix only entered the game in the second half as the left inside forward, unfortunately suffering a broken leg bone. Yesterday, the two new generals, Lie Lai and Tailai Te, played in his place, probably for training purposes, so their strength was greatly reduced. The forward line was extremely disorganized, and at crucial moments, there was a lack of coordination. The lineup was as follows:

Hayes, Asher, Turner, Ke Ke, Babu, Tailai, Baierte Lai, Lix (Lie Lai replaced him), Hixins, Lie Tailai, Kou Kehanmu

The Final Score is Five to Two In the first half, Donghua was at its peak, winning three goals. Chen Hongguang left the field due to abdominal pain at 25 minutes, fighting with ten men. Before long, Lincoln's left inside forward, Lie Lai, also left the field due to foot pain, both sides fought with ten men. Donghua's defense was tight and safe, while the forwards bravely pressed forward. First, Chen Jiaqiu scored a penalty kick, then Cao Qiuting shot from afar, and finally Chen Jiaqiu shot in front of the goal, scoring three consecutive goals. In the second half, the situation was slightly worse. Donghua's inner guards seemed to be negligent, leading to the loss of two consecutive goals in a stable situation. However, the loss of the second goal was actually due to Lincoln's left-wing Baierte Lai being in an extremely obvious offside position, but he was allowed to score directly into the net. Neither the referee nor the linesmen noticed, so Donghua's loss of this goal was extremely unfortunate. With Lincoln scoring two goals, the situation suddenly became serious. Donghua then worked harder and relied on the cooperation of the forwards, with Jiaqiu and Yutian each scoring a goal, ending the game with a score of 5-2.

Donghua's Momentum Surpasses Lincoln At 3:00 PM, referee Kelilai ordered the game to begin, with Lincoln attacking first, advancing step by step. Getting a free kick, Lu Zhongen jumped up and caught the ball, sending it to the front. Chen Jiaqiu's attack was ineffective. Wu Youliang and Cao Qiuting forced a corner kick, which Lincoln headed to clear the danger. The ball then turned to Donghua, and the corner kick was cleared. Chen Hongguang, single-handedly, went deep into the enemy territory. Lincoln's goalkeeper rushed out 15 yards and kicked the ball out first, averting the danger. However, Donghua's offensive was extremely strong, clearly above Lincoln. Qian Jingyong frequently won corner kicks, surrounding and attacking the goal, but none were successful.

Penalty Kick Opens the Record At 15 minutes, Chen Yutian sent the ball to the right, and Cao Qiuting dribbled forward. The ball touched Lincoln's left inner guard's hand, and a penalty kick was awarded. The audience immediately rejoiced, feeling proud. Chen Jiaqiu kicked the ball into the right corner of the goal, very clear, and the record was opened. Five minutes after the center kickoff, Donghua Guan Xun'an kicked an offside ball. Chen Jiaqiu received it and dribbled forward. Lincoln's goalkeeper ran out again to kick it, but the ball was obtained by Cao Qiuting, who immediately sent it to the goal. The goalkeeper ran back but had not yet settled his feet and could not turn around to save the ball. Thus, the ball was sent into the left corner of the goal by Cao, and Donghua scored two goals.

Chen Jiaqiu Records Another Achievement From then on, Donghua's momentum grew stronger, and Lincoln's defense could not defend against it. Chen Hongguang got a free kick in the enemy territory, but Qian Jingyong's pass was too wide and ineffective. Then, Chen Jiaqiu forced a corner kick, and Qian Jingyong's cross was good, but it was saved by the goalkeeper. Just as one wave subsided, another arose. Little Qian got the ball from Lincoln's right inner guard's foot and passed it in front of the goal. Chen Yutian stopped it and passed it to Jiaqiu, who lifted his foot and shot, hitting the goal again. The ball went low into the corner of the goal, very skillful. Soon, the first half ended, with Donghua winning three goals.

The Battle Resumes, and a Tragedy Occurs After the lemon juice, the game resumed. In one instance, Cao Qiuting ran forward to grab the ball and shot forcefully at the goal, but the ball went out of bounds. Lincoln then launched an attack. After several back-and-forths, Lincoln's left inside forward Lix dribbled the ball forward. Li Ning rushed forward to grab it, with great force. Lix immediately fell to the ground. Lix's foot was broken with skin and bone. He was rushed off the field and given first aid by Lincoln soldiers and officers present, before being sent for medical treatment. It is feared that he will be disabled.

Two Consecutive Goals Shock the Audience Donghua continued its fierce attack, and Lincoln's goal was under siege on all sides, with shots coming from left and right like raindrops, but many were unsuccessful. Wan Xianghua saw a high ball and headed it, but it went out of bounds again. Lincoln suddenly counterattacked, and Donghua's defense, which had been safe for a long time, suddenly became negligent. After Kou Kehanmu broke through the defense line, he passed the ball in front of the goal, and the right inside forward shot the ball, which went into the net. In less than three minutes, Lincoln's left-wing received a pass from the backfield, penetrated the defense alone, and went straight to the backfield. Wang Changying failed to stop him, and Li Ning's attempt to stop him was also ineffective, allowing him to dribble to the front of the goal and score. However, this person was already offside, but it was not penalized. Donghua lost two consecutive goals, and the audience was immediately terrified.

Chen Jia Will Serve the Country Faithfully Seeing that the situation was not good, Donghua renewed its efforts and became stronger again. Not long after Lincoln scored two goals, Chen Jiaqiu retaliated with a goal. This goal was first shot by Chen, and the goalkeeper fell to the ground and knocked the ball to the ground. The two sides fought fiercely for a long time, but Chen Jiaqiu still managed to kick it in. Chen then left the field due to abdominal pain for a short rest. He re-entered the battle five minutes later, and the audience applauded him. Chen Yutian and Wan Xianghua were also not to be outdone, cooperating and advancing together. Not far from the goal, Yutian also scored a goal. At this time, the audience shouted enthusiastically, and the sound shook the sky. After that, the two sides competed with each other, and the situation was still tense. The final whistle was blown, and Donghua won a resounding victory with a score of 5-2.

The officials of the competition are: starter Zhuang Xiangqing, chief referee Zhou Jiaqi, reporter Hong Zunsa, referees Li Xinbiao, A Erpanyi, Shi Qiangsi, Chen Yuze, Wang Fudan, chief finish judge Ling Xitao, chief timer Chen Yuehe, disciplinary committee Mei Zifan, Wu Boying, and doctor Song Guowei.

Free Talk

Aphorisms of Elder Ma Xiangbo at 93 Years Old

How Deeply Involved in Superstition and Cruelty Were We in the Past! 101

Once, Old Mr. Xiang was on the veranda of the Leshan Hall, quietly observing the myriad forms of nature, finding contentment and pleasure in himself. Suddenly, he was moved, called me to his side, and said these words:

"I think, without a proper faith, one truly doesn't know to what extent superstition and cruelty can go. Let me tell you about things from the past. Ancient people only knew of a round heaven and a square earth. Emperors built carriages, making the top round and the bottom square: This was imitating heaven, truly superstitious. One must know to revere the 'Heaven that birthed the people', the 'Heaven that sent down the people', that is, the Creator; not that tangible, visible object, the blue expanse of the sky!

What is this about heavenly yang and earthly yin, the five elements mutually overcoming each other? During the Later Han dynasty, when people built houses, they would catch a passerby, kill him, and bury the corpse under the foundation of the new house! They said it was to suppress evil spirits. Wouldn't you say that's unjust? What is this about yang being superior and yin being inferior, harming women? All sorts of inhumane acts, such as the one praised in Tang dynasty novels, where a guest remarked that the host's maidservant was beautiful, and the host then ordered the maidservant to be steamed alive and the entire corpse brought to entertain the guest: How cruel is that act?

Han Changli is considered a literary giant, but when it comes to faith, he's outdated. He initially rejected Buddhism, but ended up being devoted to it, because he fundamentally didn't understand life, what happens before death, what happens after death: Therefore, he couldn't escape that fabricated cycle of reincarnation! The way Chinese people learn Buddhism is mostly caused by having no central guiding principle.

The Neo-Confucianism of the Song and Ming dynasties, with 'Heaven is principle, nature is principle', talking about it endlessly, they couldn't even clarify a single concept! For example, saying, 'If the ruler's heart is correct, then the country will be governed'. They don't know how many stages of governing a country there are between a ruler's heart being correct and the country being governed; that one word 'then', how easy is it? They valued empty talk and lacked substance. Even those who discussed Neo-Confucianism were so confused; it's even more unknowable about others!

When will we have a proper faith, so that we can eliminate all sorts of superstitions and cruelties (')"

Slogans Printed on Mooncakes 102

— Xu Wanhua

丨A Word of Caution to Teahouse and Food Shop Owners丨

As the Mid-Autumn Festival approaches, the fervent enthusiasm for eating mooncakes is once again returning to its former state, even in this Northeast region that cannot be recovered. As you pass through those mooncake-transformed streets: the fluttering mooncake shop signs and the colorful mooncake decorations will surely evoke a sweet and juicy sensation at the bottom of your tongue. However, mooncakes were originally called 'reunion cakes', and they are meant to symbolize the celebration of reunion: now that the country is shattered and homes are in danger, I wonder what thoughts arise in people's minds when they eat mooncakes? I believe it would be best to print cautionary slogans on the mooncakes, to awaken the general public from their deep slumber. I humbly suggest the following standards:

"Remembering national crisis and celebrating the Mid-Autumn Festival, which of the two is more important?"

"The Japanese are sucking the blood of the Northeast, yet you are indulging in eating mooncakes!"

"The loss of territory is like a mooncake with a corner already missing."

"Is this the time for you to be eating mooncakes?"

"May you save a few mooncake coins to donate to the Northeast Volunteer Army."

"When you eat mooncakes, don't forget that the people of the Northeast are drinking the northwest wind!"

"You must first discuss recovering the Northeast before you can enjoy your mooncakes in peace."

"During this season of reunion, don't let our land remain broken for so long! But looking at the current mooncake trend, it seems to be a thing of the past: I wish in advance that next year, when we eat mooncakes, there won't be a second anniversary of the Northeast being lost, then these slogans of mine can also become obsolete."

Everyone's Mid-Autumn Festival 103

— Xue Fan

丨"The round moon shines on the nine provinces, some families rejoice, some families grieve: Some couples share a quilt, some wander homeless outside"!丨Nursery Rhyme丨

The volunteer soldiers in the three northeastern provinces have been fighting bloody battles against the enemy for a year, advancing wave upon wave. They have repeatedly attacked Shenyang, but ultimately withdrew due to lack of ammunition. Now, the volunteer soldiers have declared that they will attack Shenyang on the Mid-Autumn Festival to eat mooncakes. They are determined to save our dying Chinese nation with black iron, and they want to wash away our past shame with red blood. The Mid-Autumn Festival for the volunteer soldiers in the three northeastern provinces will surely be spent amidst the roar of cannons and the earth-shattering cries of battle.

The youth within the Pass who are still able to live in relative peace, seeing the bright moon in the sky and the earth like silver on Mid-Autumn Festival, truly think it is a time to enjoy themselves. Some secretly arrange to go out and enjoy the moon with their lovers, seeking hidden pleasures, joyfully awaiting the arrival of Mid-Autumn Festival to revel in the joys of life, focusing only on the smiles and tears of their lovers, and ignoring the safety of the country. The Mid-Autumn Festival for these lovers will be spent amidst such enchanting scenery.

The rich people, upon encountering the Mid-Autumn Festival, think that "How many times in life do we see the moon overhead?", how can they miss it? They are busy inviting relatives and friends to open a feast under the moon on Mid-Autumn Festival night, truly enjoying the moon. In the eyes of the rich, the Mid-Autumn Festival is naturally a delightful affair.

The poor people, due to the arrival of the Mid-Autumn Festival, are besieged by creditors demanding repayment everywhere, relentlessly pressing for it, and unable to cope. Not only do they not get to taste any mooncakes or ginkgo nuts, but they only see more of the world's fickleness and coldness! In the eyes of the poor, the Mid-Autumn Festival is naturally a dead end.

Every Mid-Autumn Festival, the farmers all look delighted because there is always a considerable harvest in the fields. The farmers get a share of harvest for their labor, a glass of wheat wine, and happily spend the farmers' Mid-Autumn Festival on the banks of the fields.

In recent years, due to the economic depression, industry and commerce have declined sharply, factories have closed one after another, and most of the workers have lost their jobs. Now the Mid-Autumn Festival has arrived again, and I don't know how many more shops and factories will close down? Society will have another batch of unemployed people who are in distress and have no one to turn to. What a terrible impression the Mid-Autumn Festival is on these people whose jobs are precarious?

Lamenting to General Jiang and General Cai, Pillars of Respect, in Light of the Emergency in Rehe

Another report of emergency in Rehe. I truly cannot bear to speak of it. Who will resist for a long time? For years, the country has lost its defensive barriers. Like beans and stalks, we are brothers. But slaves will become descendants. When will we call on Jiang and Cai? To rekindle the national spirit.

Glad to Hear of Progress by the Volunteer Army in the Three Northeastern Provinces

The invaders have been here for another year. My eyes are filled with wounds, weeping tears. The quail's head (eastern territory) was given to Qin, yet they are drunk. At the wine table, I am still sober while grieving for Ying. From now on, how can there be a hidden sky? Who will execute the righteous with a white horse? Happily, the patriots of Guandong (Manchuria) are listening, fighting to kill the enemy and avenge the times.

This is a True Story 104

— Ke Ding'an

丨Jesus Conquers the Devil?丨

I am a non-religious person. This Sunday, I accepted an invitation from a colleague at school to go to the Jesus Church next door for worship. The pastor stood and preached the Bible. After preaching the Bible, they sang hymns. After doing this devoutly, they followed it with silent prayer: After doing it several times in the same way, a sound of 'Amen' signaled the end of the service. Just at this moment, earth-shattering noises erupted outside the door.

"I don't want to go in. If I go in, I will have no place to stay. I can't get through this door no matter what..."

Several of the younger people who were worshiping rushed outside to see what was happening. They realized that the one shouting was a young woman, but she was extremely frantic. Next to her were several female church members, holding her back. She simply refused to go in. Fortunately, Pastor Zhao came up with a wonderful idea. He took out a Bible and told her to look at it. She said:

"Two roads... it's so difficult for me! ... It's so difficult for me!" She finally said this and was guided into the Jesus Church by the Bible.

The onlookers and church members crowded around her. As for her, she was baring her fangs and claws, as if resenting being forced to come in. Her eyes were wide open, like a pair of copper bells, and she looked terrified!

The two female church members who accompanied her briefly described her situation to the audience:

"She is from Shaoxing. Because she couldn't bear the abuse of her grandmother-in-law, she hanged herself when she really couldn't take it anymore. When her grandmother-in-law saw her handling her final affairs, she also imitated her. However, they were rescued by the people living with them. Her husband, because he was unemployed at home, saw the unsettling situation and actually hanged himself. Later, her grandmother-in-law remarried her. Now her former husband has been looking for her for several months. We think that Jesus can conquer everything, so we asked her to come to worship. If she believes in the church, her former husband will probably not come looking for her again!"

After she attended the service once, she regained her original kind state. The location of the Jesus Church is Wuzhen, Zhejiang.

Silver Threads (15) 105

— Jiang Hongjiao

(8)

Fenruo felt such great joy and gratitude that a huge flower of laughter bloomed in her heart, but she couldn't stop the tears from flowing like a mineral spring. Her ancient well of over ten years was dry and silent, devoid of life. She never imagined that this elementary school teacher who sat guarding the green carpet would transform into a valiant warrior, and moreover, a hero fighting the enemy for the country; she even less imagined that he would find her again, pleading with her; she even suspected whether he had really abandoned his wife, whether he had not yet married a new, graceful and wealthy wife, whether he really wanted to take an old widow back? She didn't know how she should allow him or reject him. She repeatedly deliberated, thinking for the sake of his future happiness, reputation, and career, that she should definitely not allow him to go with him, and that she should sacrifice herself no matter what. She lay on the table, sobbing unrestrainedly and grievingly.

"Fen, don't cry! I can tell you some sincere words. The grand welcome ceremony cannot move my heart; I only beg you in sorrow to give me some joy, to let my heart, which has longed for and wandered aimlessly for over ten years, find a settlement, to let my immensely passionate emotions, and the wings of my heart, which have been barely covering them, have a chance to cover my heart again! Ah! My good Fenruo! I know your previous ideals and admirations, so I escaped to join the army, and now I have achieved my goal; moreover, your husband has been dead for over ten years, your family is also gone, your beautiful emotions are still the same as before, please have pity on me, comfort me, so that I can complete the unfinished career, settle the unsettled heart, have pity on me." When Regiment Commander Yuan spoke, he had no military accent, but was as gentle as a lamb, and he was indeed using sincerity to touch Fenruo's heart.

"Really? Really?" Fenruo, listening as if hypnotized, really stopped crying, raised her face, looked at Regiment Commander Yuan, feeling very excited and happy, "But, what method will I use to prove that your words are completely reasonable? What method will I use to test whether society's non-opposition to your actions is correct? If I do as you say, how will I analyze my own actions, so that they are not mistaken?"

"Fenruo, my good girl!" Regiment Commander Yuan became even more impassioned and excited.

"Eh! Where am I still a good girl?" Fenruo was a little surprised, suspecting that he dared to deliberately tease her.

"This is my subjective view, my intuition, I truly still regard you as a good girl, and moreover, as a supreme celestial being,"

I beg you, please trust that my words are completely reasonable, and completely correct; if you allow it, then your actions will not be wrong at all, your thoughts will be completely accurate."

"But you are too unfair to your former wife."

"There's no way around it; moreover, her whereabouts are now unknown."

"What if you meet her again in the future? How will you deal with it? This is closely related to your reputation and career, you should consider it carefully."
