Speech

Good Luck is Unreliable 106

— Hou Ying

In this era of flourishing science, without real knowledge, one cannot create any great cause. In other words, a great cause cannot be created by someone without knowledge.

Looking at the great inventors of the past and present, which one did not have real knowledge, which one did not have decades of real research? It can be said that none of them succeeded by chance.

In ancient times, when two generals faced each other in battle, if one of them was defeated, then he would take out his final, best skill, chanting incantations, wanting to borrow the magic weapon of his ancestor or master. But in the end, he could never defeat the enemy. Similarly, in today's ball games, if one is unwilling to practice diligently beforehand, but hopes that the best player on the enemy team will suddenly get injured and be taken to the hospital during the game, I believe that this kind of thinking is the decline of personality and the decay of thought.

There are also some people who worry that they cannot afford a high-level education because they don't have money. I say, that doesn't matter. Even like our country's Mencius, and the West's Edison, which of them had money in their youth? I can even say that most great inventors don't have money. As long as we work hard and practice diligently, the problem of not having money simply cannot be established.

No, I want to say, "The strength of the country must have real knowledge. Good luck cannot lead to success."

Literature and Art

Gifting the Autumn Moon 107

— Ze Ji

Duckweed and catkins on the road to the end of the world, suddenly meeting again, each surprised, asking how I am, still drifting like a broken stem, cheering that you have already become a father, the days ahead are vast, the days past are full of sorrow, carelessly bearing the head of youth, all things are better than enjoying life, life is fleeting and youth is old, riding a horse, willow branches brush the clothes, in the winding corridors, often forgetting the scheming, the articles to serve the country are now decayed, what do we have in our lives, endless concern for old friendships, walking and singing in the faint smoke and fragrant grass, envying your indifference and willingness to taste the world, I am truly lacking peace in my heart.

Science

Petroleum 108

— Shao Liang

Petroleum, known as PETROLEUM in the West, is a liquid fuel, which is much better than solid fuels such as coal, because it is not only easy to ignite, but also has no residue. When burning, just inject it into the oil storage area, and use a pipe to lead it to the flame outlet, then you can continue to ignite it without any effort. From this point of view, petroleum is indeed a very good fuel! Although all countries in the world produce oil, the United States and Russia produce the most. Although my country's Shaanxi, Gansu, Xinjiang, and Sichuan produce petroleum, there is no large-scale exploitation, which is not enough for domestic application, so that foreign oil is sold in our country. According to the latest survey, about 101,522,842 barrels are used each year. If this huge drain is not remedied, it is a pity!

There are two methods of extraction: manual and mechanical. When using the manual method, manpower is used to dig deep wells in various parts of the coalfield. When the location of the petroleum is reached, a pump is used to suck it out, store it in a large tank, and send it to the refinery. When using the mechanical method, a high frame is first erected on the oil field, with an iron pulley connected to a lever and an iron cone iron rod. Then, the force of the machine is used to drive the lever, causing the iron cone to lift up and fall, drilling the oil field into a deep well, and then the oil can be extracted.

Petroleum is a brownish liquid, which is formed by ancient animals and plants undergoing crustal movement, buried in the soil underground, subjected to great pressure from above, and without air circulation, and decomposed by bacteria for a long time. If it is placed in an iron steamer and heated with fire, when the heat reaches 150 degrees Celsius, the gas that is steamed out will turn into gasoline when it encounters cold. When heated to 300 degrees Celsius, the gas that is steamed out will turn into kerosene when it encounters cold. When heated to 360 degrees Celsius, the gas that is steamed out will turn into heavy oil when it encounters cold.

Gasoline (VOLATILE OIL) is a colorless and transparent liquid, its properties are very soft, and its ignition temperature is very low, so it cannot be used for lighting. But it can remove oil stains from clothes and utensils and be used as fuel in machinery.

Kerosene (KERASENE) is a yellow liquid, its calorific value is very high, and it is easy to burn. If it is sealed in a cylinder, it will not change or rot, and there is no risk of self-ignition, because of these advantages, it is used for lighting and for repelling pests.

Page 16

Heavy Oil (HEAVY OIL) is a pale yellow, pasty liquid that is difficult to ignite. Machine oil (MECHANIC OIL) and paraffin (PARAFFIN) can be extracted from this oil. Machine oil is a viscous liquid. If it is applied to the axles of machines, it can reduce friction and can also be used as fuel for cars and warships. Paraffin is a white crystalline solid that melts when heated and is also very easy to burn. It can be used to make candles and wax paper.

Gasoline and heavy oil cannot be used for lighting. Why can kerosene be used for lighting? This is because gasoline ignites too quickly, which is very dangerous. Heavy oil ignites too slowly, which is less dangerous but difficult to ignite, so gasoline and heavy oil cannot be used for lighting. As for kerosene, the ignition is moderately fast, it is easy to ignite, the danger is less, and it can be completely burned, so kerosene can be used for lighting.

How can gasoline remove dirt? This is because it can dissolve oily substances, causing it to gradually evaporate, so oil stains on clothes and utensils can be removed with gasoline.

Forbidden Meat 109

Social Improvement Discussion Group

Proposal to Abolish School's Weekly Holiday 110

— Zhen Zhi

In our country, where biology is backward, education is bankrupt, and everything lags behind others, it is natural to imitate the things of other advanced countries. But even though we imitate, we should not blindly follow, but should choose the good and follow it, and change the bad.

The motivation for drafting this article is that I saw Mr. Fo's article "A Bill for Children's Studies" in yesterday's "Tan Yan" column of this journal and was moved to write it. However, I am only taking the issue of weekly holidays out separately for everyone to discuss, so it can be said that this proposal of mine is a proposal, or it can be said to be a supplement to Mr. Fo's opinion. However, Mr. Fo's article was not published in this association.

The school's weekly holiday, in the final analysis, has a bit of a certain religious color. European customs are brought along with it. Our authorities do not investigate its advantages and disadvantages and rashly imitate it until now. I really don't know what it means to leave this kind of inferior trail here at a time when it is clear that a certain religion is a tool for imperialist cultural aggression and anesthetic thought, and when the call to overthrow it is being sung loudly. As for saying that it is because of six days of diligent study and that one day of holiday is used to compensate for the loss of mental energy, it is close to sporadic efforts and as contradictory. (A person's mental energy is valued for daily exercise and daily rest.) Because people use their mental energy for seven or eight hours every day, one or two hours of exercise, or one or two hours of leisurely gazing and walking, is enough to restore the depleted mental energy, and there is plenty of time to spare. Why create the evils of movie theaters and dance halls with this one day of time and waste useful learning? Our country has reached a time when studying is necessary to save the country, and science is necessary to save the country. I think everyone agrees with my words, so I solemnly put forward this case for detailed discussion. There are also places that have the same meaning as Mr. Fo, so I will not repeat them.

Letter to the Editor 111

Mr. Rui Yucheng, I read your masterpiece (Fabric Printing Method) in the supplement of the Shen Bao on the ninth of this month. I know that you have a lot of research in science. Now I have the following things to ask you to teach.

There are many kinds of pigments on the market, some of which can be dissolved in water and dyed, such as direct, salt-based, and acidic pigments. I tried to print them on cotton fabrics and saw that the colors were very bright and lovely, but unfortunately they fade.

I am a layman when it comes to science, but I need a lot of this kind of pigment every year. Now I want to print it on cotton fabrics to make the colors not fade. Alas, sir, I have spent several months of effort researching this color, but the result is always that it cannot reach a durable and non-fading state. This is a big drawback in my experience, and I don't have any suitable friends to guide me at the moment. Reading your masterpiece, I know that you are also very proficient in dyeing. I hope you can give me a reply in the supplement, that is my greatest gratitude.

My address is in Sheng Maolong Dyehouse, Nanshi, Datuan Town, Pudong. Please answer my request no matter what. You know that I am now looking forward to your good news. Wishing you progress, Sheng Sanmin, 9, 11.

Market News 112

Xiaodongmen Xie Da Xiang Promotes Domestically Produced Silk and Satin Xiaodongmen Xie Da Xiang Silk Fabric Store has long been recognized by society for its exquisite goods and low prices. Recently, in order to thoroughly resist inferior goods, all goods displayed in the store are marked with their country of origin to facilitate customer purchases. It is also actively promoting domestic goods and has set up a silk and satin department to vigorously promote them. There are daily sales of discounted goods, so customers are extremely crowded, it is said.

The Rise of Domestically Produced Socks and Garters Socks and garters, although a small item of clothing, have a very wide consumption. Chinese people neglect it because it is small, so inferior goods are everywhere in the market. According to the customs report, last year it was worth hundreds of millions of yuan, and the rights and interests flowed out, which is a pity to see. Since September 18th, Chinese people have finally awakened from a dream and paid a little attention to this. At that time, the first to create the Asia America Socks and Garters Company was Mr. Wen, a well-known figure in the Shanghai business community, who set up a manufacturing factory with a certain scale and gradually improved it. Now it has been completed. The quality of its fineness and the beauty of its style are really above the inferior goods and are on par with the famous American Paris suspenders. It is truly a highlight of domestic goods. The sales points are Sincere, Wing On, Sun Sun, Lihua, China, and major stores. The general manager's office is Nanyang Socks Factory on Nanjing Road, Shanghai.
